I will relay the messages between the players.\n\n2. `move(ICON_ID, X_COORD, Y_COORD)` — to move an icon to a specified location with their `(X_COORD, Y_COORD)` coordinates, according to the coordinate system in the picture on the left. I will move the icons for you and give you visual feedback.
